Running End-to-End tests

This notebook generates URLs AND runs tests manually. These tests can be run “offline” via the github runner using .github/workflows/run-benchmarks.yml.

from datetime import datetime
import subprocess
import sys
import warnings
warnings.filterwarnings('ignore')
sys.path.append('..')
from helpers.eodc_hub_role import fetch_and_set_credentials
credentials = fetch_and_set_credentials()
envs = ['dev', 'feature']
results_stores
['s3://nasa-eodc-data-store/tile-benchmarking-results/dev_2023-11-17_01-07-52/',
 's3://nasa-eodc-data-store/tile-benchmarking-results/feature_2023-11-17_01-09-35/']
results_stores = []
for env in envs:
    subprocess.run(["rm", "-rf", "results/"])
    subprocess.run(["rm", "-rf", "urls/"])    
    subprocess.run(["mkdir", "urls/"])
    subprocess.run(["python", "gen_test_urls.py", "--env", env, "--numurls", "10", "--datasets", "external"])
    subprocess.run(["sh", "./run-tests.sh", "10", f"https://{env}-titiler-xarray.delta-backend.com"])
    current_datetime = datetime.now().strftime('%Y-%m-%d_%H-%M-%S')
    results_store = f's3://nasa-eodc-data-store/tile-benchmarking-results/{env}_{current_datetime}/'
    results_stores.append(results_store)
    subprocess.run(["aws", "s3", "cp", "results/", results_store, "--recursive"])
